    window.Adomik = window.Adomik || {};
    Adomik.randomAdGroup = function() {
        var rand = Math.random();
        switch (false) {
            case !(rand < 0.09): return "ad_ex" + (Math.floor(100 * rand));
            case !(rand < 0.10): return "ad_bc";
            default: return "ad_opt" + (Math.floor(10 * rand));
        }
    };
</script>

    <script>
        var disabledClass = 'maps-buttons-inactive';
        var activeClass = 'maps-buttons-active';

        var searchIdentifier = "london";

        function getSearchOptions() {

            var placeholder = $('input#keywords').attr('placeholder');
            var keywords    = $('input#keywords').val();

            if (keywords == placeholder) keywords = '';

            var data = {
                q: $('input#location').val(),
                section: "for-sale",
                category: "residential",
                price_frequency: "per_month",
                include_shared_accommodation: '',
                keywords: keywords
            };

            if (searchIdentifier) {
                data['identifier'] = searchIdentifier;
            }

            if ($('form#form-search-and-refine.is-new-refine').length > 0) {
                $('form#form-search-and-refine select').not('.none').each(function() {
                    var name = this.name,
                        val  = $(this).find('option:selected').val();

                    if (name === 'shared_ownership') {
                        if (val === 'only') {
                            name = 'is_shared_ownership';
                            val  = 'true';
                        } else if (val === 'exclude') {
                            name = 'is_shared_ownership';
                            val  = 'false';
                        } else if (val === 'include') {
                            name = 'include_shared_ownership';
                            val  = 'true';
                        }
                    } else if (name === 'retirement_homes') {
                        if (val === 'only') {
                            name = 'is_retirement_home';
                            val  = 'true';
                        } else if (val === 'exclude') {
                            name = 'is_retirement_home';
                            val  = 'false';
                        } else if (val === 'include') {
                            name = 'include_retirement_homes';
                            val  = 'true';
                        }
                    }

                    if (!data[name]) {
                        data[name] = val;
                    }

                });
            } else {
                $('form#form-search-and-refine select').not('.none').each(function() {
                    if (!data[this.name]) {
                        data[this.name] = '';
                    }

                    data[this.name] = $(this).find('option:selected').val();
                });
            }

            $('form#form-search-and-refine input[type=checkbox]:checked').not('.none').each(function() {
                if (typeof this.value != 'undefined') {
                    if (!data[this.name]) {
                        data[this.name] = [];
                    }

                    data[this.name].push($(this).val());
                }
            });

            $('#search-listings-filters a.facet-link-active').each(function() {
                var val = $(this).attr('data-value');
                if (typeof val != 'undefined') {
                    var name = $(this).attr('data-param');

                    if (!data[name]) {
                        data[name] = new Array();
                    }

                    data[name].push(val);
                }
            });

            // this is to handle the various include_* arguments that appear in the url
            if (!data['is_retirement_home'] && !data['include_retirement_homes']) {
                data['include_retirement_homes'] = 'true';
            }

            if (!data['is_shared_ownership'] && !data['include_shared_ownership']) {
                data['include_shared_ownership'] = 'true';
            }

            if (!data['new_homes']) {
                data['new_homes'] = 'include';
            }


            return data;
        }

        $('select[name=price_frequency]').on('change', function() {
            $('#rent_attributes').find('select:not(.none) option:selected').prop("selected", false);
        });

        $('select[name*=_min]').on('change', function() {

            var $searchField = $(this).data('search-field'),
                $max_select  = $(this).parents('.search-refine-element-panel').find('select[name*=' + $searchField + '_max]').not(':disabled'),
                $max_options = $max_select.find('option'),
                $max_chosen  = parseFloat( $max_select.find('option:selected').val() ),
                $min_chosen  = parseFloat($(this).val()),
                $clone       = $(this).find('option:gt(0)').clone(false); // clone the min list (excluding the first option)

            if (!isNaN($min_chosen)) {

                // minimum amount selected

                if (!$max_select.find('option[value="' + $min_chosen + '"]').val()) { // max option list have these values

                    $max_select.html($clone).prepend($max_options.eq(0)); // recreate max list
                    $max_select.find('option[value="' + $max_chosen + '"]').prop('selected', true); // retain the selected max option

                }

                // this removes all options that are less than the minimum selected
                $max_select.find('option').each(function() {

                    if ($(this).val() === '') {

                        return true;

                    }

                    if ($(this).val() < $min_chosen) {

                        $(this).remove();

                    }
                }).end();

                if ($max_chosen) {

                    $max_select.find('option[value="' + $max_chosen + '"]').prop('selected', true);

                }

            } else {

                // no min selected - min and max should show full lists
                $max_select.html($clone).prepend($max_options.eq(0));

                if (!isNaN($max_chosen)) {

                    $max_select.find('option:selected').removeAttr('selected');
                    $max_select.find('option[value="' + $max_chosen + '"]').prop('selected', true);

                }

            }
        });
        $('select[name*=_min]:not(.none)').trigger('change');

        $(document).ready(function() {

            

            load_script('https://m.zoocdn.com/www/ub/zoopla/static/scripts/widgets/listings/results-8b2409193d.js');
            load_script('https://m.zoocdn.com/www/ub/zoopla/static/scripts/widgets/listings/relevant-agents-3e60b079d3.js');

            
var isAlert = false,
    isAlertModified = false,
    pageSize = "100",
    view = "list";

var alerts = ZPG.user_alerts({
    isAlert: isAlert,
    isAlertModified: isAlertModified,
    pageSize: pageSize,
    view: view
});

$(document).on('click', '[data-alert=create], [data-alert=modify]', function (e) {

    e.preventDefault()

    var $this = $(this),
        action = $this.attr('data-alert'),
        href = $this.attr('data-href');

    // Don't do anything if disabled
    if ( typeof disabledClass !== 'undefined' && $this.hasClass( disabledClass) ) {
        return false;
    }

    // Create or modify alert
    alerts.init( action, href );

});


            if ( ZPG.support.sessionStorage() ) {

    var session = window.sessionStorage,
        tally   = session.getItem('srpViews') || 0,
        close   = session.getItem('alertsPopupClose') || 0;


        if (parseInt(ZPG.util.getParameterByName('pn')) >= 2) {
            tally++;
            session.setItem('srpViews', tally);
        }
        if (tally && close != 1) {
            $('#alerts-popup').show();
        }


}

$( ".js-alerts-popup-btn-close" ).on( "click", function( e ) {

    e.preventDefault();
    $( "#alerts-popup" ).hide();
    close++;
    session.setItem( "alertsPopupClose", close );

});

$( ".js-alerts-popup-btn-create" ).on( "click", function( e ) {

    close++
    session.setItem( "alertsPopupClose", close );

});



            
    load_script('https://m.zoocdn.com/www/ub/zoopla/static/scripts/external/jquery-71d0a960da.sticky-kit.min.js', function() {

        <script>
        (function() {
            function createCookie(name, value, nrOfDays) {
                var expires,
                    currentDate,
                    calculateTime;

                if (nrOfDays) {
                    currentDate = new Date();
                    calcMsFromDays = nrOfDays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
                    currentDate.setTime(currentDate.getTime() + calcMsFromDays);
                    expires = ' ;expires=' + currentDate.toGMTString();
                } else {
                    expires = '';
                }
                document.cookie = name + '=' + value + expires + '; path=/;domain=zoopla.co.uk';
            }

            messageData =  'We use cookies to give you the best possible experience on our site, and so that we and third parties can show you more personalised ads, including adverts on other websites. By clicking "Accept", you agree to our use of cookies. '

            var fragment = document.createDocumentFragment(),
                elBody = document.getElementsByTagName('BODY')[0],
                elFirstChild = elBody.firstChild,
                elWrap = document.createElement('div'),
                elHolder = document.createElement('div'),
                elCopy = document.createElement('p'),
                elLink = document.createElement('a'),
                elButton = document.createElement('button'),
                messageText = document.createTextNode(messageData),
                buttonText = document.createTextNode('Accept'),
                linkText = document.createTextNode('Find out more');


            elWrap.setAttribute('class', 'cookie-banner');

            elWrap.classList.add('is-rwd');

            elHolder.setAttribute('class', 'container-wrap');
            elCopy.setAttribute('class', 'cookie-banner__copy');
            elLink.setAttribute('href', '/privacy/cookies');
            elLink.setAttribute('target', '_blank');
            elLink.setAttribute('rel', 'noopener noreferrer');
            elLink.setAttribute('class', 'cookie-banner__link');
            elButton.setAttribute('class', 'button');
            elButton.setAttribute('type', 'button');
            elButton.setAttribute('title', 'Agree to our use of cookies');
            elButton.classList.add('cookie-banner__button');

            elLink.appendChild(linkText);
            elButton.appendChild(buttonText);
            elCopy.appendChild(messageText);
            elCopy.appendChild(elLink);

            elHolder.appendChild(elCopy);
            elHolder.appendChild(elButton);
            elWrap.appendChild(elHolder);
            fragment.appendChild(elWrap);

            document.body.insertBefore(fragment, elFirstChild);

            elButton.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                elWrap.classList.add('js-cookie-accepted');
                elLink.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
                elButton.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
                createCookie('cookie_policy_acceptance', '1', 365);
            });
        })();
    </script>

    


        <script>
    (function() {
        var subNavs = [].slice.call(document.getElementsByClassName('subnav')),
            subNavTriggers = [].slice.call(document.getElementsByClassName('has-subnav')),
            openSubNavToggles = [].slice.call(document.querySelectorAll('.mnav__item--expands .has-subnav')),
            closeNavToggles = [].slice.call(document.getElementsByClassName('mnav__toggle--main-close')),
            backNavToggles = [].slice.call(document.getElementsByClassName('mnav__toggle--subnav-close')),
            openNavToggle = document.getElementsByClassName('mnav__toggle--main-open')[0],
            accessibleSubnavItems = [].slice.call(document.querySelectorAll('.mnav__item--expands [class^="subnav__link"]')),
            subnavControls = [].slice.call(document.querySelectorAll('.subnav__controls a')),
            zooplaProButtons = [].slice.call(document.querySelectorAll('.subnav--agents .button')),
            accessibleAccountLinks = [].slice.call(document.querySelectorAll('.notifications__link')),
            initialViewPortWidth = window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWindth,
            isTouchEnabled = 'ontouchstart' in document,
            activeClass = 'js-active',
            expandedClass = 'js-expanded',
            noScrollClass = 'js-noscroll',
            tappedClass = 'js-tapped',
            hasOrientationChanged = false;

        [].push.apply(accessibleSubnavItems, subnavControls);
        [].push.apply(accessibleSubnavItems, zooplaProButtons);

        function throttle(fn, delay) {
            if (typeof fn !== 'function') {
                return;
            }

            var lastCall = 0;
            delay = typeof delay === 'number' ? delay : 100;

            return function() {
                var now = +new Date();

                if (now - lastCall < delay) {
                    return;
                }

                lastCall = now;
                fn.apply(this, arguments);
            }
        }

        function closeNav() {
            [].slice.call(document.getElementsByClassName(expandedClass)).forEach(function(el) {
                el.classList.remove(expandedClass);
            });

            updateAccessibilityForSubnav(false, accessibleAccountLinks);

            document.body.classList.remove(noScrollClass);
        }

        function resetNavigation(isSmallScreen) {
            if (isSmallScreen) {
                closeNav();
            }
        }

        // unfortunately IE will still complain about using
        // el.classList.contains('some-class') on SVG elements
        function hasClass(element, cls) {
            return (' ' + element.className + ' ').indexOf(' ' + cls + ' ') > -1;
        }

        // hide subnav for large screens
        function hideSubnavigation() {
            var activeEl = document.getElementsByClassName(activeClass)[0];

            if (activeEl) {
                activeEl.classList.remove(activeClass);
            }
        }

        function expandSubnav(e) {
            updateAccessibilityForSubnav(true, accessibleSubnavItems);
            e.preventDefault();
            e.target.nextElementSibling.classList.add(expandedClass);
        }

        function toggleDisplayOfSubnav(e) {
            if (e.target.offsetTop > 0) {
                e.target.previousElementSibling.classList.toggle(activeClass);
            } else {
                e.target.previousElementSibling.classList.remove(activeClass);
            }
        }

        function addToggleToSubnavItems(isSmallScreen) {
            if (subNavs.length) {
                subNavs.forEach(function(el) {
                    if (!isSmallScreen) {
                        el.addEventListener('mouseenter', toggleDisplayOfSubnav, false);
                        el.addEventListener('mouseleave', toggleDisplayOfSubnav, false);

                    } else {
                        el.removeEventListener('mouseenter', toggleDisplayOfSubnav, false);
                        el.removeEventListener('mouseleave', toggleDisplayOfSubnav, false);
                    }
                });
            }
        }

        function handleTap(e) {
            var thisEl = e.target,
                wasTapped = thisEl.classList.contains(tappedClass);

            if (e.type === 'touchstart' && !wasTapped) {
                e.preventDefault();

            } else if (e.type === 'touchend') {
                if (wasTapped) {
                    thisEl.classList.remove(tappedClass);

                } else {
                    subNavTriggers.forEach(function(el) {
                        if (el.classList.contains(tappedClass)) {
                            el.classList.remove(tappedClass);
                        }
                    });

                    thisEl.classList.add(tappedClass);
                    e.preventDefault();
                }
            }
        }

        function handleTouchEnabledNav(isSmallScreen) {
            if (isTouchEnabled && subNavTriggers.length) {
                subNavTriggers.forEach(function(el) {

                    if (!isSmallScreen) {
                        el.addEventListener('touchstart', handleTap, false);
                        el.addEventListener('touchend', handleTap, false);
                    } else {
                        el.removeEventListener('touchstart', handleTap, false);
                        el.removeEventListener('touchend', handleTap, false);
                    }
                });
            }
        }

        function addAccessToSubnav(isSmallScreen) {
            if (openSubNavToggles.length) {
                openSubNavToggles.forEach(function(el) {

                    if (isSmallScreen) {
                        el.addEventListener('click', expandSubnav, false);

                        if (!el.hasAttribute('title')) {
                            el.setAttribute('title', 'Opens sub navigation');
                        }

                    } else {
                        el.removeEventListener('click', expandSubnav, false);

                        if (el.hasAttribute('title')) {
                            el.removeAttribute('title');
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
        }

        function updateAccessibilityForSubnav(isSmallScreen, items) {
            if (items.length) {
                items.forEach(function(el) {
                    if (isSmallScreen) {
                        el.removeAttribute('tabindex');
                    } else {
                        el.setAttribute('tabindex', '-1');
                    }
                });
            }
        }

        function updateNavForScreenSize(isInitialLoad) {
            var viewportWidth = window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWindth,
                smallBreakpoint = 960,
                isSmall = viewportWidth <= smallBreakpoint;

            hideSubnavigation();

            if (isInitialLoad === true || hasOrientationChanged || initialViewPortWidth !== viewportWidth) {
                addAccessToSubnav(isSmall);
                resetNavigation(isSmall);
                addToggleToSubnavItems(isSmall);
                updateAccessibilityForSubnav(false, accessibleSubnavItems);
                handleTouchEnabledNav(isSmall);
            }
        }

        // Prepare subnavigation and accessibility features
        // if the screen size matches criteria

        updateNavForScreenSize(true);

        // Add event listeners

        window.addEventListener('resize', throttle(updateNavForScreenSize));

        window.addEventListener('orientationchange', function() {
            hasOrientationChanged = true;
        }, false);

        window.addEventListener('beforeunload', hideSubnavigation, false);

        document.addEventListener('touchstart', function(){}, true);

        document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            var hasExpanded = document.getElementsByClassName(expandedClass)[0],
                isChildOfExpanded = hasExpanded && hasExpanded.contains(e.target),
                isExpanded = hasClass(e.target, expandedClass),
                isOpenNavToggle = openNavToggle ? 
                    openNavToggle === e.target || openNavToggle.contains(e.target) :
                    false;

            if (isOpenNavToggle || isChildOfExpanded || isExpanded) {
                return;
            }

            closeNav();

        }, false);

        if (openNavToggle) {
            openNavToggle.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                document.getElementById('main-nav').classList.toggle(expandedClass);
                document.body.classList.add(noScrollClass);
                updateAccessibilityForSubnav(true, accessibleAccountLinks);
            }, false);
        }

        if (closeNavToggles.length) {
            closeNavToggles.forEach(function(el) {
                el.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    closeNav();
                }, false);
            });
        }

        if (backNavToggles.length) {
            backNavToggles.forEach(function(el) {
                el.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    updateAccessibilityForSubnav(false, accessibleSubnavItems);
                    e.preventDefault();
                    document.querySelector('.subnav.js-expanded').classList.toggle(expandedClass);
                }, false);
            });
        }
    })();
</script>


        <script>

            function page_onload() {
                

    

    ZPG.util_textarea.init();



            }

            window.onload = page_onload;

        </script>



        

               <div id="dfp-1x1-0" class="dfp-banner dfp-banner-1x1">

    <script>

        if (typeof googletag !== 'undefined') {
            googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display('dfp-1x1-0'); });
        }

    </script>

</div>



    </body>

</html>
